GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_z*A**c5/(c6*A**c7 + c8)

I need to find a candidate that can match the GT:
$$-0.2092A^2 + \frac{0.2153A^2}{0.9716A^4 + 1} - 0.2092A \exp(-0.06535t)$$

The GT has three terms:
1. $-0.2092A^2$ (polynomial in A)
2. $\frac{0.2153A^2}{0.9716A^4 + 1}$ (rational function of A)
3. $-0.2092A\exp(-0.06535t)$ (exponential decay in t, times A)

Let me check each candidate systematically for structural compatibility.

**Candidate 2:** $A^3c_0 + \frac{A^2c_1}{(A+c_2)^2} + A^2c_3 + \frac{Ac_4}{(c_5+t)^5} + c_6 + c_7\exp(A^{c_8}c_9)$

The term $\frac{A^2c_1}{(A+c_2)^2}$ with $c_2=0$ gives $c_1$, a constant — not $A^2/(A^4+1)$. The exponential decay term $A\exp(-kt)$ isn't here. No match.

**Candidate 46:** Similar issues with $1/(c_5+t)^5$ instead of $\exp(-t)$.

**Candidate 45:** $\frac{A^{3/2}c_0}{A+c_1} + \frac{\sqrt{A}c_2}{A+c_1} + \frac{A^6c_3 t^{c_4}}{A+c_1} + \frac{A^5c_5 t^{c_4}}{A+c_1} + \frac{Ac_6}{A+c_1} + \frac{Ac_7\exp(c_8 t)}{A+c_1} + \frac{c_9\exp(c_8 t)}{A+c_1}$

Setting $c_1=0$: terms become $A^{1/2}c_0, A^{-1/2}c_2, A^5c_3t^{c_4}, A^4c_5t^{c_4}, c_6, c_7\exp(c_8t), c_9A^{-1}\exp(c_8t)$. Not helpful.

**Candidate 47:** $A^3c_0 + \frac{A^2c_1}{(A+c_2)^2} + A^2c_3 + A^2c_4 + Ac_5 + \frac{Ac_6}{(c_7+t)^5} + c_8$

No exponential in t. No match.

**Candidate 17:** $A^3c_0 + A^3c_1\exp(c_2 t) + \frac{A^2c_3}{(A+c_4)^2} + A^2c_5 + \frac{Ac_6}{(c_7+t)^5} + c_8$

Setting $c_0=0$: has $A^3\exp$, not $A\exp$. No.

**Candidate 45 revisited with general $c_1$:** The rational structure $A/(A+c_1)$ gives $\frac{A^2}{A+c_1}$ type terms, not $\frac{A^2}{A^4+1}$.

None of these candidates have a term like $\frac{A^2}{A^4+\text{const}}$ or equivalently $\frac{A^2}{A^4c + c'}$, which requires $A^4$ in the denominator. Let me search for $A^2/(A^2+c)$ type terms.

**Candidate 15:** $\frac{A^2c_0}{A^2+c_1} + Ac_2 + c_3\sin(Ac_4+c_5) + c_6 + c_7\exp(A^{c_8}c_9)$

Setting $c_3=0, c_7=0$: gives $\frac{A^2c_0}{A^2+c_1} + Ac_2 + c_6$. This has $A^2/(A^2+c_1)$, not $A^2/(A^4+c)$. These are structurally different. But wait — can $c_7\exp(A^{c_8}c_9)$ approximate $-0.2092A^2$? No, exponentials aren't polynomials.

After exhaustive checking, none of the candidates contain a rational term with $A^4$ in the denominator combined with $A\exp(ct)$. The GT's rational term $A^2/(A^4+1)$ is structurally unique and not reproducible by any candidate.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK22)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_z*A**c5/(c6*A**c7 + c8)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.2092*A^2 + 0.2153*A^2/(0.9716*A^4 + 1) - 0.2092*A*exp(-0.0654*t)`

The GT has three terms:
1. A term proportional to `A^2`
2. A rational function `A^2/(c*A^4 + 1)` 
3. A term `A*exp(-kt)` with time dependence

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

**Key structural requirements:**
- Must have `A^2` polynomial term
- Must have `A^2/(A^4 + const)` rational term
- Must have `A*exp(-ct)` term
- No other basis functions (sin, log, etc.) unless they can be zeroed out

For candidates with `sin`, `log`, `cos`, or other transcendental functions that can't be zeroed without losing essential terms, they won't match.

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** Has `A^5*t`, `A*`, `log(A^5*exp(...)+1)` terms. The structure involves `log` and `A^5` terms divided by `(c1+c2*exp(c3*t))`. This doesn't simplify to the GT structure. The log terms can't produce `A^2/(A^4+1)`.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `A^3*c0 + A^2*c1/(A+c2)^2 + A^2*c3 + A*c4/(c5+t)^5 + c6 + c7*exp(A^c8*c9)`. Has `A^3` (can set c0=0), `A^2/(A+c2)^2` which is NOT `A^2/(A^4+1)`, time dependence is `1/(c5+t)^5` not `exp(-ct)`, and `exp(A^c8*c9)` is exponential in A, not the rational function needed. Cannot match.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `A^c0*c1 + c2*sin(A*c3+c4) + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8+c9*t)+1)`. The `log(c7*exp(A*c8+c9*t)+1)` is a softplus-like function, not `A^2/(A^4+1)`. Can't produce the rational function.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `A^5*c0*t + A^5*c1 + A*c2 + A^c3*c4 + c5 + c6*exp(A^c7*c8)`. No rational function `A^2/(A^4+1)`, no `exp(-ct)` term. Can't match.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*exp(c1*t)*sin(A*c2+c3) + c4*log(c5*exp(A*c6+c7*t)+1)`. Sin and log/softplus functions. Can't produce `A^2` or `A^2/(A^4+1)`.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `c0 + c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(A*c4) + c5*exp(A*c6) + c7*log(A^c8*c9+1)`. Exponentials in A, log in A, exp in t. No `A^2` polynomial, no rational function.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `A*c0/(c1+t)^2 + c2*exp(c3*t)*sin(A*c4+c5) + c6*log(c7*exp(A^2*c8+c9*t)+1)`. The time-dependent term `A/(c1+t)^2` is not `A*exp(-ct)`. The log/softplus can approximate but not exactly equal `A^2/(A^4+1)`. Sin term present.
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** `A^c0*c1 + c2*sin(A*c3+c4) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t)*sin(A*c8+c9)`. Sin functions can't produce `A^2/(A^4+1)`. No rational function.
Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** `c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c4*exp(A^c5*c6) + c7*log(A^5*c8*exp(c9*t)+1)`. Sin, exp in A, log. Can't match.
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10:** `A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6 + c7*exp(A^c8*c9)`. Has `exp(c5*t)` but not `A*exp(ct)`. Sin and exp(A^c) can't produce rational function.
Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 11:** `A^c0*c1 + c2*sin(A*c3+c4) + c5 + c6/(c7+c8*exp(c9*t))`. The time term `1/(c7+c8*exp(c9*t))` is not `A*exp(-ct)`. Missing A dependence in time term.
Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 12:** Similar to Candidate 2 with sin added. Same issues.
Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]
